  var input, filter, table, tr, td, i, txtValue;

      }

data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p>The tournament will be held in the following location:</p><p style="text-align: center;"><b>Charlotte Convention Center</b><br />501 S College St<br />Charlotte, NC 28202, USA</p></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-40b51f9 elementor-widget elementor-widget-google_maps" data-id="40b51f9" The tournament starts thereafter with the Day 1 Swiss rounds. Seniors and Juniors start 30 minutes later.</p><p>Players qualified to Day 2 must be in the venue by <b>21 January at 8:30 am EST</b> (13:30 UTC) for the team checks. The Day 2 Swiss rounds (if any) and the top cut will be played thereafter.</p></div></div></div></div></div></section><section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-d8ffa24 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="d8ffa24" data-element_type="section"><div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default"><div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-1ea33c6" data-id="1ea33c6" data-element_type="column"><div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated"><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7921af7 elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="7921af7" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-spacer"><div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ec2bb11 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="ec2bb11" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><div class="title" style="font-weight:500">Prizes</div></h2></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ca9294b elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="ca9294b" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p>This event is part of the <a href="https://victoryroadvgc.com/2024-season-structure/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2024 official TPCi circuit</a> and thus <b>it rewards Championship Points</b> (CPs).</p><p>As a participation goodie, all players will be provided a Pokémon Regional Championships <b>promo card</b>, an event <b>playmat</b>, <b>promo</b> and <b>badge</b>, a regional <b>lanyard</b> and a <b>pen</b>. Players can also purchase:</p><ul><li>“Stage 1 Package”, which adds an event T-shirt and two side-event tickets to the goodies;</li><li>“Stage 2 Package”, which further adds an event dice, pin and bag, a notebook and two additional side-event tickets; or</li><li> “VIP Package”, which further adds a VIP static seating during main event, access to the VIP room, access to the Wi-Fi password, a badge with name, and an event backpack.</li></ul><p>Additionally, the best-placed players will receive the following <b>CPs</b> and <b>prize money</b> depending on final attendance:</p></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-1ee5047 elementor-tabs-view-horizontal elementor-widget elementor-widget-tabs" data-id="1ee5047" data-element_type="widget" given as a choice of scholarship (in all cases) or cash (for minors, as a Pokémon Visa<sup>®</sup> Prepaid Card). For lower prizes, it will be given as cash (for minors, as a Pokémon Visa<sup>®</sup> Prepaid Card).</p></div></div></div></div></div></section><section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-54fbd9b elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="54fbd9b" data-element_type="section"><div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default"><div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-543cce1" data-id="543cce1" data-element_type="column"><div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated"><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d3f435a elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="d3f435a" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-spacer"><div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f67732e elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="f67732e" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><div class="title" style="font-weight:500">Overview</div></h2></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-8f7ff55 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="8f7ff55" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p>The <b>Charlotte Regional Championships</b> is an official TPCi Regional-level event for Pokémon VGC, TCG and <i>Pokémon GO</i>. It is the seventh Regional-level event of the <a href="https://victoryroadvgc.com/2024-season-calendar/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2024 season</a> in the North American circuit.</p><p>The ruleset is <a href="https://victoryroadvgc.com/2024-rules-regulations/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>VGC Regulation Set F</b></a>, and it is played using <b>open team lists</b>. The <b>clause banning Dragon Cheer</b> due to a bug in ver. 3.0.0 of <i>Pokémon Scarlet</i> &amp; <i>Pokémon Violet</i> is in effect for this event.</p></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-b5d16b9 elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="b5d16b9" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-spacer"><div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a5d6333 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="a5d6333" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><h3 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><u><i>A little bit of history</i></u></h3></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d6da158 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="d6da158" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p>The <b>United States</b> has been part of the North America region of the official TPCi circuit since the very beginning, also being home to the TPCi headquarters. It has hosted multiple major events, including Regional Championships, old-era National Championships, all editions of the North America International Championships and <b>most World Championships</b> (only excluding 2013, 2022 and 2023). The United States&#8217; greatest VGC success are the four World Championship wins achieved by <a href="https://twitter.com/RayRizzoVGC" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Ray Rizzo</b></a> (2010, 2011 and <a href="https://youtu.be/VVwpu4tCsWo" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2012</a>) and <a href="https://twitter.com/WolfeyGlick" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Wolfe Glick</b></a> (<a href="https://www.pokemon.com/us/play-pokemon/worlds/2016/teams/masters/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2016</a>), not even counting being the home country of <b>6</b> Senior Division and <b>5</b> Junior Division World Champions too.</p><p>The most recent tournament held in the <b>United States</b> was the <a href="https://victoryroadvgc.com/2024-portland/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2024 Portland Regional</a>, played in the VGC Regulation Set E earlier in the same month. The finals saw 2-time Regional Champion <a href="https://twitter.com/LexiconVGC" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Alex Underhill</b></a> defeat 2024 Toronto Regional Champion <a href="https://twitter.com/ChuppaVGC" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Chuppa Cross IV</a> to win his third Regional Championship title!</p><p>The last time there was an event in <b>North Carolina </b>was the <a href="https://victoryroadvgc.com/2023-charlotte/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2023 Charlotte Regional</a>, played in the VGC Regulation Set B in March 2023. The <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vk4dk1LsL4Y&amp;t=23706s" target="_blank" rel="noopener">finals</a> saw 2016 Worlds quarter-finalist <a href="https://twitter.com/AzazeL_the_God" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Justin Carris</b></a> defeat then one-time Regional Champion <a href="https://twitter.com/JoeUX9" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Joseph Ugarte</a> to win his first Regional Championship title!</p></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-71a6a80 elementor-hidden-desktop elementor-hidden-tablet elementor-hidden-mobile elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="71a6a80" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p>American <a href="https://twitter.com/TheKingVillager" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>James Evans</b></a>, the <a href="https://www.pokemon.com/us/play-pokemon/worlds/2018/vgc-seniors/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2018 Senior Division World Champion</a>, defeated Brazilian <a href="https://twitter.com/AgatiGa" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gabriel Agati</a> in the NAIC finals.</p></div></div></div></div></div></section><section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-7a278b2 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="7a278b2" data-element_type="section"><div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default"><div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-f0075db" data-id="f0075db" data-element_type="column"><div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated"><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-522a83b elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="522a83b" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-spacer"><div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-96cc646 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="96cc646" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><div class="title" style="font-weight:500">Sign-up instructions</div></h2></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-17aed1a elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="17aed1a" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p>Sign-ups for the event are done through <a href="https://rk9.gg/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">RK9 Labs</a> platform, and you will first need to set up your <a href="https://rk9.gg/profile" target="_blank" rel="noopener">RK9 profile</a> and have a <a href="https://sso.pokemon.com/sso/login?locale=en&amp;service=https://club.pokemon.com/us/pokemon-trainer-club/caslogin" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Play! Pokémon Player ID</a>. All players must comply with the <a href="https://assets.pokemon.com//assets/cms2/pdf/play-pokemon/rules/play-pokemon-covid-19-protocols-07112023-en.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Play! Pokémon COVID-19 Protocols</a>.</p><p>Sign-ups are <b>$69 </b>(+ $5.10 tax), and they open on <b>21 November at 7 pm EST</b> (22 November at 00:00 UTC). There are <b>864 spots</b> for Masters players and 60 spots for Senior and Junior players.</p><ul><li>A second wave was later announced to open on <b>7 December at 7 pm EST</b> (8 December at 00:00 UTC). There are 20 new spots for Senior and Junior players.</li></ul></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ff28cef elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="ff28cef" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-button-wrapper">
<a href="https://rk9.gg/tournament/CHA2pGWrNLxBnP8EuHex" target="_blank" class="elementor-button-link elementor-button elementor-size-sm" role="button">

<span class="elementor-button-icon elementor-align-icon-left">
<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-gamepad"></i>			</span>
<span class="elementor-button-text">Sign-ups sold out!</span>
</span>
</a></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4137e04 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="4137e04" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p><b>Spectator</b> passes are <b>$15</b> (+ $1.15 tax) and can be purchased <a href="https://rk9.gg/spectator/pokemon-charlotte-2024" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>here</b></a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div></section></div></div></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-73e433e elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="73e433e" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-spacer"><div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></section></div></div></div></div><div class="site-footer"><div data-elementor-type="footer" data-elementor-id="18531" class="elementor elementor-18531 elementor-location-footer" data-elementor-settings="[]"><div class="elementor-section-wrap"><section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-d72bf11 elementor-hidden-phone elementor-hidden-tablet elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="d72bf11" data-element_type="section" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;gradient&quot;}"><div class="elementor-background-overlay"></div><div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default"><div class="elementor-column elementor-col-33 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-1c3da84" data-id="1c3da84" data-element_type="column"><div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated"><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-696052f elementor-widget elementor-widget-image" data-id="696052f" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="image.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container">
